[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m436[0m[39m:    public [0m[1;35mCompressorStreamFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m437[0m[39m:        this.decompressUntilEof = null;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m438[0m[39m:        this.memoryLimitInKb = [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m439[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m440[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Introduce a sane default memory‐limit in CompressorStreamFactory  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Define a new constant [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. DEFAULT_MEMORY_LIMIT_IN_KB = [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m * [0m[1;36m1024[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCompressorStreamFactory.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Change the no-arg constructor from setting memoryLimitInKb = [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m to [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemoryLimitInKb = DEFAULT_MEMORY_LIMIT_IN_KB.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Preserve the existing overloaded constructor [0m[1;39m([0m[39mboolean, int[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m so that callers [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwho explicitly pass a limit continue to work.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Document the new default:  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In CompressorStreamFactory Javadoc, note that callers using [0m[1;35mgetSingleton[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout an explicit memory limit will now be capped at DEFAULT_MEMORY_LIMIT_IN_KB. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Provide guidance on how to supply a higher or lower limit via the public [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mCompressorStreamFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mboolean, int[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m API.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOptional enhancement[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Clamp maxCodeSize in ZCompressorInputStream  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Although the default-limit fix prevents OOM, it’s good practice to reject absurd[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode sizes even if a huge limit is configured. In the ZCompressorInputStream [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconstructor, after deriving maxCodeSize from the header, add:  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize > MAX_SUPPORTED_CODE_SIZE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Unsupported LZW code size: "[0m[39m + maxCodeSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Where MAX_SUPPORTED_CODE_SIZE is, for example, [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi.e. [0m[1;36m65536[0m[39m entries[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. This [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextra guard prevents runaway loops if future code changes bypass the memory check. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Rationale and side effects  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – By moving from “no check” [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m-1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to a large but bounded default [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m MiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwe eliminate the unbounded allocation path that led to the OOM under fuzzing.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Consumers who need more than the default can still request a higher [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemoryLimitInKb, preserving backward‐compatible API behavior.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – No changes are made to any harness, fuzzing logic, or test code. We only touch[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCompressorStreamFactory and optionally add a small header check in [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mZCompressorInputStream.  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Existing functionality for standard archives [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich use small maxCodeSize [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalues[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains unaffected, as they typically need far less than [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m MiB for table [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minitialization.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – If a user legitimately needs >[0m[1;36m64[0m[39m MiB, they must explicitly supply that via the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mCompressorStreamFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mboolean, int[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m constructor, which is already supported.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – This approach avoids adding broad exception catches or modifying utility code [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbeyond the intended factory path.  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Relevant code ranges to patch  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   <code_range>src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/compressors/CompressorStre[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mamFactory.jav[0m[1;92ma:436[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m440[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   <code_range>src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/compressors/CompressorStre[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mamFactory.java:[0m[1;39m[[0m[39madd new DEFAULT_MEMORY_LIMIT_IN_KB constant near top[0m[1;39m][0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m> [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   <code_range>src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/compressors/z/ZCompressorI[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnputStream.java:[0m[1;39m[[0m[39moptional, around lines [0m[1;36m82[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m83[0m[1;39m][0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
